 ) a half marathon was organized today from the Jawaharlal Nehru Stadium in the capital Delhi
 duniyabar ke kai nami athleton ne nauveen airtel half marathon main shirkat kar apana damakham dikhaaya
 Yes
 lakshmananan or prija shridharan ravivaar ko yojit airtel dilli half marathon main awwal bhartiya purush or mahila athlete rahe
 Starting from Jawaharlal Nehru Stadium, the marathon ended here with Atesdu Sagee of Ethiopia and Florence Kiplagat of Kenya
 sege ne 210,000 dollar inami is res main 59 minute 12 second samay ke saath nayaa course record banaaya or saal 2008 main ithiopia ke hi deribe merga dwaara banaae gaye 59 minute 15 second ke course ricard ko tod diya
 Florence, on the other hand, won the women's section by finishing the race in one hour and eight minutes
 bharat ke purush athleton main lakshmananan ne ek ghanta chaar minute or 44 second samay ke saath 15waan sthaan hasil kiya
 He topped the Indians
 lakshmananan ko puraskaar ke taur par 2
 Received Rs 5 lakh
 khet ram duusare or ratti ram tisare sthaan par rahe
 Olympic runner Preza completed the race in one hour 20 minutes 04 seconds
 kavita raut ek ghante 20 minute 09 second samay ke saath duusare or lalita babbar ek ghante 20 minute 09 second samay ke saath hi tisare sthaan par raheen
 Lalita has been the best female athlete for India before
 bharat kii ore se mahila varg main maujuuda champion sudhaa singh chauthe kram par raheen
 She reached the finish line 16 seconds later from first-placed Preza
 prija ne mahila varg main kul 15waan sthaan hasil kiya
 Over 31 thousand people participated enthusiastically in the Half Marathon
 marathon main kai namchin filmi sitaron ne bhi shirkat kii
 During this time, the enthusiasm of Delhi was being seen
 
 In the 100 meters, former Olympic and world champion Donovan Bailey was appointed as the 'event Ambassador'
 flying sikh naam se mashhoor purv bhartiya trek va field sprinter milkha singh is aayojan ke 'khel atithi' hai

 aayojan kii suraksha vyavastha main yatayaat police ko kanoon-vyavastha banaae rakhane ke liye 800 nijee surakshakarmiyon ke alaava 1000 swayamsevak apana sahyog dene main jute rahe

 jaankaree ke mutabik ghatana sthal par kareeb 60 pulisavaale maujuud hai or raahat kaa kaam teji se jari he

 pune main 'maratha kranti morcha' ne railway trek jam kar diya he

 is andolan ke maddenjar maharashtra ke siem devendra fadanvis ne baithak bulaai he
 All ministers will be involved in this meeting
 bataa den, maratha samudaay ke liye aarakshan kii maang ko lekar chal rahaa rajyavyapee pradarshan hinsak hone ke baad maharashtra ke mukhyamantri devendra fadanvis ne is puure maamle par bayaan diya tha
 He said that the government has taken cognizance of the opposition of the Maratha community and has taken several decisions on it
 sarkaar unase baat karne ke liye taiyaar he
 He said that the government had enacted a law for the reservation of Maratha community, but the Bombay High Court had imposed a stay on it
 isse pehle, pradarshnakariyon ke patharav main ek consteble kii maut ho gai jabaki nau anya jakhmi ho gaye
 The Mumbai bandh was called by the Maratha Kranti Morcha on Wednesday
 iske baad mumbai main kai jagahon par best bason par patharav kiya gaya
 Trains were stopped in Thane
 lekin buudhvaar kii dopaher tak hinsa tej hote dekh maratha kranti morcha ne mumbai band waapas le liya tha
 According to the 'maratha Kranti Morcha', if the government did not take a proper decision in favor of the Marathas, public outrage would spread unrest throughout Maharashtra
 iske jimmedaar sirf or sirf mukhyamantri honge
 The Marathas have already made it clear not to talk
 siem ke baatcheet ke prastaav ko buudhvaar ko maratha samaaj ne thukraa diya tha
 The Maratha community is 30 percent, for the politically influential Maratha community, the matter of reservation is a very controversial issue

 ’’ isamen party netritv par ek tarah se sawaal uthaate hue kaha gaya he, ‘‘matadaataaon ko aakarshith karne ke liye mul vichaardhaaratmak muddon or siddhanton ke saath netritv kii vishwasaneeyata kii jarurat hoti he

 ’’ Panchajanya's editorial also cautioned against taking a tough stance towards the BJP and its leadership that if the party did not correct itself, it would not do well in the upcoming Lok Sabha elections

 centurian main khele gaye is match main toss harkar pehle ballebaaji karte hue team india ne south africa ke saamne 189 ranon kaa lakshya rakhaa

 south africa ne captain je pi dumini ke naabad 64 ranon kii badaulat yah jeet darj kii he

 south africa kii taraf se henrik classen ne 30 gendon main tabadatod 69 ranon kii pari kheli, jabaki captain jepi dumini ne 40 ball main naabad 64 ran banaae or chakka lagaakar team ko jeet dilaai
 South African batsman Heinrich Klassen was adjudged 'man of the Match'
 bharat kii ore se jayadev unadakat ko 2 wicket or pandya-shardul ko 1-1 wicket hasil hua
 The scoreboard LIVE dhoni-pandey gave India a target of 189 for Africa, batting first, Team India scored 188 runs losing 4 wickets in 20 overs and set a target of 189 runs in front of South Africa
 team india kii taraf se manish pandey ne apane tii-20 kariyar kii duusari fifty jadte hue shandaar 79 ranon kii pari kheli
 While MS Dhoni also scored 52 runs while pushing the second T20 Fifty
 bhartiya team ke opening ballebaaj rohit sharma ko junior daalaa ne khaataa kholane kaa mauka bhi nahin diya or elbeadblu out kar pavilion kaa rasta dikhaaya
 Subsequently, Suresh Raina (30) shared a 44-run partnership with Shikhar Dhawan (24), but South Africa captain JP Duminy did not let the partnership freeze
 dumini kii gend par lanbaa shot maarane kii koshish main dhawan farhaan behardian ke haathon lapke gaye
 After the dismissal of Dhawan, skipper Virat Kohli (1), who came to support Raina, did not support him
 vah daalaa kii gendbaaji main funs kar rah gaye or gend wicket ke peeche khadey henrik classen ke haathon main thama baithe
 According to the agency, the Indian team had lost their three wickets at a score of 45
 aise main pandey ummid kii kiran banakar maidan par utre
 He shared a 45-run partnership for the fourth wicket with Raina on the basis of the required batting and brought the team to a score of 90
 haalanki, yahaan apni lay talash rahe raina ko fehulakavayo ne 90 ke score par hi elbeadblu out kar bharat kaa chauthaa wicket bhi gira diya
 Pandey, meanwhile, scored his second half-century of his T20 career with a single off the last ball of the 15th over
 pandey ne iske baad dhoni ke saath yahaan se team kii pari ko sambhala 98 ranon kii shandaar saajhedaari kar 20 overon main team kaa score 188 tak pahunchaaya
 Dhoni and Pandey remain unbeaten
 is pari main pandey ne 48 gendon main chah chauke or teen chakke lagaae, vahiin dhoni ne bhi apane tii-20 kariyar doosraa ardhashatak puraa kiya

 is pari main south africa ke liye junior daalaa ne do wicket liye, vahiin dumini or fehulakavayo ko ek-ek safalataa mili
 India got the first batting in the second T20 match, South Africa captain JP Duminy decided to bowl after winning the toss in the second consecutive match and invited Team India to bat first
 bhartiya team ne ek badlaav kiya
 Jasprit Bumrah has a stomach problem, so Shardul Thakur was given a chance
 south africa ne koi badlaav nahin kiya
 Recently, the GST Council has reduced the GST rate on affordable housing properties under construction from 8 percent to 1 percent and for the non-affordable housing segment under other construction properties it has been reduced from 12 percent to 5 percent
 haalanki nai daron kaa matlab he ki developers ab input tex credit kaa laabh nahin le sakate hai
 This includes projects whose booking is done before April 1, 2019
 1 april, 2019 se shuru hone vaale nae project ke liye anivaary rup se nai daren lagu hongi
 This decision has been taken in the council meeting chaired by Finance Minister Arun Jaitley last week
 jiesti kii daron main kii gai yah katautee ghar kharidne waalon ke liye ek badi saugat he
 This gives both developers and buyers a chance to celebrate
 aise main jab maang or aapurti donon morche par is sector main dabaav kii sthiti bani hui he
 The developers have built houses, but there are no buyers in the market
 yani, makaanon kii aapurti to he, lekin uski maang main narmi he
 In such a situation, this step of the government is a relief for the house buyers as well as the developers
 baithak main kifayati awaas kii paribhaasha main bhi badlaav hua
 The GST Council has fixed the price for a property to be included under Affordable Housing up to a maximum of 45 lakhs
 saath hi metro shaharon (dilli ensiaar, mumbai, chennai, kolkata, bangaluru, hyderabad) main 60 varg meter (646 varg feet) kaa karpet aria or anya jagahon par 90 varg meter (969 varg feet) nirdhaarit kiya he
